#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, gc
os.environ["MPLBACKEND"] = "Agg"

import cv2
import numpy as np
import threading
import gymnasium as gym
from gymnasium.wrappers import TimeLimit
from gymnasium import ObservationWrapper, spaces
from collections import deque

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import torch.optim as optim
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

# Fix for NumPy bool8 deprecation
if not hasattr(np, 'bool8'):
    np.bool8 = bool

#  Preprocessing wrapper 
class PreprocessFrame(ObservationWrapper):
    """
    Applies, in order:
      1) grayscale
      2) crop bottom 20px
      3) resize to 8484
      4) normalize [0,1]
    """
    def __init__(self, env):
        super().__init__(env)
        orig = env.observation_space
        # single channel 8484
        self.observation_space = spaces.Box(
            low=0.0, high=1.0, shape=(84, 84), dtype=np.float32
        )

    def observation(self, obs):
        # obs: HWC (2101603)
        gray   = cv2.cvtColor(obs, cv2.COLOR_RGB2GRAY)     # 210160
        crop   = gray[:190, :]                             # drop bottom 20px
        resized= cv2.resize(crop, (84, 84), interpolation=cv2.INTER_AREA)
        return (resized.astype(np.float32) / 255.0)        # [0,1]

#  FrameStack fallback 
class FrameStack(gym.Wrapper):
    def __init__(self, env, num_stack):
        super().__init__(env)
        self.num_stack = num_stack
        self.frames    = deque(maxlen=num_stack)
        shp = env.observation_space.shape  # e.g. (84,84)
        self.observation_space = spaces.Box(
            low=0.0, high=1.0,
            shape=(num_stack, *shp),
            dtype=np.float32
        )

    def reset(self, **kwargs):
        out = self.env.reset(**kwargs)
        obs, info = out if isinstance(out, tuple) else (out, {})
        for _ in range(self.num_stack):
            self.frames.append(obs)
        return np.stack(self.frames, 0), info

    def step(self, action):
        out = self.env.step(action)
        if len(out) == 5:
            obs, rew, term, trunc, info = out
            done = term or trunc
        else:
            obs, rew, done, info = out
        self.frames.append(obs)
        return np.stack(self.frames, 0), rew, done, info

#  RL setup 
device = torch.device("mps" if torch.backends.mps.is_available() else "cpu")

HYPERPARAMS = {
    "PongNoFrameskip-v4": dict(
        ENV_NAME="PongNoFrameskip-v4", NUM_WORKERS=2, MAX_EPISODES=6000,
        UPDATE_INTERVAL=5, GAMMA=0.99, LR=3e-4, HIDDEN_SIZE=128,
        ENTROPY_COEF=0.01, SUCCESS_THRESHOLD=18.0
    ),
    "LunarLander-v3": dict(
        ENV_NAME="LunarLander-v3", NUM_WORKERS=2, MAX_EPISODES=2000,
        UPDATE_INTERVAL=20, GAMMA=0.999, LR=3e-4, HIDDEN_SIZE=256,
        ENTROPY_COEF=0.01, SUCCESS_THRESHOLD=200.0
    )
}

ep_counter   = 0
ep_lock      = threading.Lock()
update_lock  = threading.Lock()
rewards_hist = None
optimizer    = None
global_model = None

def make_env(name):
    env = gym.make(name, render_mode="rgb_array" if "Pong" in name else None)
    env = TimeLimit(env, max_episode_steps=1000)
    if "Pong" in name:
        env = PreprocessFrame(env)
        env = FrameStack(env, num_stack=4)
    return env

def env_reset(env):
    out = env.reset()
    return (out[0], out[1]) if isinstance(out, tuple) else (out, {})

def env_step(env, action):
    out = env.step(action)
    if len(out) == 5:
        obs, rew, term, trunc, info = out
        done = term or trunc
    else:
        obs, rew, done, info = out
    return obs, rew, done, info

class ActorCritic(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, obs_shape, n_actions, is_atari=False):
        super().__init__()
        if is_atari:
            c, h, w = obs_shape
            self.conv = nn.Sequential(
                nn.Conv2d(c, 32, 8, stride=4), nn.ReLU(),
                nn.Conv2d(32, 64, 4, stride=2), nn.ReLU(),
                nn.Conv2d(64, 64, 3, stride=1), nn.ReLU()
            )
            fc_in = 64 * 7 * 7
        else:
            self.conv = nn.Identity()
            fc_in = obs_shape[0]

        hidden = HYPERPARAMS["PongNoFrameskip-v4" if is_atari else "LunarLander-v3"]["HIDDEN_SIZE"]
        self.fc     = nn.Sequential(nn.Linear(fc_in, hidden), nn.ReLU())
        self.policy = nn.Linear(hidden, n_actions)
        self.value  = nn.Linear(hidden, 1)

    def forward(self, x):
        x = x.to(device)
        h = self.conv(x)
        if h.dim() > 2:
            h = h.view(h.size(0), -1)
        h = self.fc(h)
        return torch.softmax(self.policy(h), dim=-1), self.value(h)

class Worker(threading.Thread):
    def __init__(self, wid, name, model):
        super().__init__()
        self.wid   = wid
        self.name  = name
        self.model = model

    def run(self):
        global ep_counter, rewards_hist, optimizer
        env = make_env(self.name)
        p   = HYPERPARAMS[self.name]

        while True:
            with ep_lock:
                if ep_counter >= p["MAX_EPISODES"]:
                    env.close()
                    return
                ep_counter += 1
                ep = ep_counter

            state, _ = env_reset(env)
            buf_s, buf_a, buf_r = [], [], []
            total_reward = 0.0

            for t in range(1, 10000):
                sv = torch.from_numpy(state).float().to(device)
                with update_lock:
                    probs, _ = self.model(sv.unsqueeze(0))
                action = probs.multinomial(1).item()

                nxt, r, done, _ = env_step(env, action)
                total_reward += r
                buf_s.append(sv); buf_a.append(action); buf_r.append(r)

                if t % p["UPDATE_INTERVAL"] == 0 or done:
                    R = 0.0
                    if not done:
                        with torch.no_grad():
                            _, vn = self.model(
                                torch.from_numpy(nxt).float().to(device).unsqueeze(0)
                            )
                            R = vn.item()

                    returns = []
                    for rew in reversed(buf_r):
                        R = rew + p["GAMMA"] * R
                        returns.insert(0, R)
                    returns = torch.tensor(returns, device=device, dtype=torch.float32)
                    std = returns.std()
                    returns = (returns - returns.mean()) / (std + 1e-8) if std > 1e-6 else returns - returns.mean()

                    states  = torch.stack(buf_s)
                    actions = torch.tensor(buf_a, dtype=torch.int64, device=device)

                    with update_lock:
                        probs, values = self.model(states)
                        dist    = torch.distributions.Categorical(probs)
                        logp    = dist.log_prob(actions)
                        adv     = returns - values.squeeze()

                        actor_loss  = -(logp * adv.detach()).mean()
                        critic_loss = adv.pow(2).mean()
                        entropy     = dist.entropy().mean()
                        loss        = actor_loss + 0.5*critic_loss - p["ENTROPY_COEF"]*entropy

                        optimizer.zero_grad()
                        loss.backward()
                        nn.utils.clip_grad_norm_(self.model.parameters(), 0.5)
                        optimizer.step()

                    buf_s, buf_a, buf_r = [], [], []

                state = nxt
                if done:
                    rewards_hist[ep-1] = total_reward
                    print(f"Worker[{self.wid}] Ep {ep} Reward {total_reward:.1f}", flush=True)
                    break

def train_and_evaluate(p):
    global ep_counter, rewards_hist, optimizer, global_model

    name = p["ENV_NAME"]
    print(f"\n=== Training {name} ===", flush=True)

    ep_counter   = 0
    rewards_hist = [0.0] * p["MAX_EPISODES"]
    torch.manual_seed(42); np.random.seed(42)

    tmp_env = make_env(name)
    obs_shape = tmp_env.observation_space.shape
    n_actions = tmp_env.action_space.n
    is_atari  = "Pong" in name
    tmp_env.close()

    global_model = ActorCritic(obs_shape, n_actions, is_atari).to(device)
    optimizer    = optim.Adam(global_model.parameters(), lr=p["LR"])

    workers = [Worker(i, name, global_model) for i in range(p["NUM_WORKERS"])]
    for w in workers: w.start()
    for w in workers: w.join()

    avg_r = np.mean(rewards_hist); max_r = np.max(rewards_hist)
    print(f"\n{name} training done: avg {avg_r:.2f}, max {max_r:.2f}", flush=True)

    # Plot training curve
    plt.figure(figsize=(10,6))
    plt.plot(rewards_hist, label="Episode Reward")
    plt.title(f"{name} Training Rewards")
    plt.xlabel("Episode"); plt.ylabel("Total Reward")
    plt.grid(); plt.legend()
    plt.savefig(f"{name}_training.png")
    print(f"Saved plot: {name}_training.png", flush=True)

    # (You can add evaluation here if desired)
    torch.save(global_model.state_dict(), f"a2c_{name}.pth")
    print(f"Model saved: a2c_{name}.pth", flush=True)

    return rewards_hist

if __name__ == "__main__":
    for nm in HYPERPARAMS:
        train_and_evaluate(HYPERPARAMS[nm])

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import torch
import gymnasium as gym
import numpy as np
import cv2
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
from collections import deque
from gymnasium import spaces
from gymnasium.wrappers import TimeLimit

# Device
device = torch.device("mps" if torch.backends.mps.is_available() else "cpu")

class PreprocessFrame(gym.ObservationWrapper):
    def __init__(self, env):
        super().__init__(env)
        self.observation_space = spaces.Box(low=0.0, high=1.0, shape=(84, 84), dtype=np.float32)

    def observation(self, obs):
        gray = cv2.cvtColor(obs, cv2.COLOR_RGB2GRAY)
        crop = gray[:190, :]
        resized = cv2.resize(crop, (84, 84), interpolation=cv2.INTER_AREA)
        return resized.astype(np.float32) / 255.0

class FrameStack(gym.Wrapper):
    def __init__(self, env, num_stack=4):
        super().__init__(env)
        self.num_stack = num_stack
        self.frames = deque(maxlen=num_stack)
        shp = env.observation_space.shape
        self.observation_space = spaces.Box(low=0.0, high=1.0, shape=(num_stack, *shp), dtype=np.float32)

    def reset(self, **kwargs):
        obs, info = self.env.reset(**kwargs)
        for _ in range(self.num_stack):
            self.frames.append(obs)
        return np.stack(self.frames, axis=0), info

    def step(self, action):
        obs, reward, terminated, truncated, info = self.env.step(action)
        self.frames.append(obs)
        return np.stack(self.frames, axis=0), reward, terminated or truncated, info

class ActorCritic(torch.nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, obs_shape, n_actions):
        super().__init__()
        c, h, w = obs_shape
        self.conv = torch.nn.Sequential(
            torch.nn.Conv2d(c, 32, 8, stride=4), torch.nn.ReLU(),
            torch.nn.Conv2d(32, 64, 4, stride=2), torch.nn.ReLU(),
            torch.nn.Conv2d(64, 64, 3, stride=1), torch.nn.ReLU()
        )
        fc_input_dim = 64 * 7 * 7
        self.fc = torch.nn.Sequential(torch.nn.Linear(fc_input_dim, 512), torch.nn.ReLU())
        self.policy = torch.nn.Linear(512, n_actions)
        self.value = torch.nn.Linear(512, 1)

    def forward(self, x):
        x = x.to(device)
        x = self.conv(x)
        x = x.view(x.size(0), -1)
        x = self.fc(x)
        return torch.softmax(self.policy(x), dim=-1), self.value(x)

def evaluate(model_path="a2c_PongNoFrameskip-v4.pth", env_name="PongNoFrameskip-v4", num_episodes=10):
    env = gym.make(env_name, render_mode=None)
    env = TimeLimit(env, max_episode_steps=1000)
    env = PreprocessFrame(env)
    env = FrameStack(env, num_stack=4)

    obs_shape = env.observation_space.shape
    n_actions = env.action_space.n

    model = ActorCritic(obs_shape, n_actions).to(device)
    model.load_state_dict(torch.load(model_path, map_location=device))
    model.eval()

    rewards = []
    for ep in range(num_episodes):
        obs, _ = env.reset()
        total_reward = 0
        done = False
        while not done:
            obs_tensor = torch.from_numpy(obs).unsqueeze(0).float().to(device)
            with torch.no_grad():
                probs, _ = model(obs_tensor)
            action = probs.squeeze().multinomial(num_samples=1).item()
            obs, reward, done, _ = env.step(action)
            total_reward += reward
        rewards.append(total_reward)
        print(f"Episode {ep+1}: Reward = {total_reward}")

    avg = np.mean(rewards)
    print(f"\nAverage Reward over {num_episodes} episodes: {avg}")

    # --- Plot the reward graph ---
    plt.figure(figsize=(10, 6))
    plt.plot(rewards, marker='o', linestyle='-')
    plt.title(f"A2C Evaluation Rewards on {env_name}")
    plt.xlabel("Episode")
    plt.ylabel("Total Reward")
    plt.grid(True)
    plt.savefig("a2c_evaluation_rewards.png")
    print("Saved plot: a2c_evaluation_rewards.png")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    evaluate()
